<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=apple&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200"></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/apple" class="extiw" title="w:apple">apple</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/apple" class="extiw" title="w:apple">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Apple_red_delicius_flower_end.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Apple_red_delicius_flower_end.jpg/220px-Apple_red_delicius_flower_end.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="230" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Apple_red_delicius_flower_end.jpg/330px-Apple_red_delicius_flower_end.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Apple_red_delicius_flower_end.jpg/440px-Apple_red_delicius_flower_end.jpg 2x" data-file-width="848" data-file-height="888"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Apple_red_delicius_flower_end.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>A red apple</div></div></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=apple&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/appel#Middle_English" title="appel">appel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/%C3%A6ppel#Old_English" title="ppel">ppel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote"></span><span class="mention-gloss">apple, fruit in general, ball</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote"></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-West_Germanic/applu" title="Reconstruction:Proto-West Germanic/applu">*applu</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/aplaz" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/aplaz">*aplaz</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote"></span><span class="mention-gloss">apple</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote"></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco"><a href="/wiki/aipple#Scots" title="aipple">aipple</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href="/wiki/apel#West_Frisian" title="apel">apel</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/appel#Dutch" title="appel">appel</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/Apfel#German" title="Apfel">Apfel</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href="/wiki/%C3%A4pple#Swedish" title="pple">pple</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href="/wiki/%C3%A6ble#Danish" title="ble">ble</a></i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h%E2%82%82%C3%A9b%C5%8Dl" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/hbl">*hbl</a></i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h%E2%82%82%C3%A9bl%CC%A5" class="mw-redirect" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/hbl">*hbl</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote"></span><span class="mention-gloss">apple</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote"></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Welsh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Welsh language">Welsh</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy"><a href="/wiki/afal#Welsh" title="afal">afal</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Irish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Irish language">Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ga"><a href="/wiki/%C3%BAll#Irish" title="ll">ll</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt"><a href="/wiki/obuolys#Lithuanian" title="obuolys">buols</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href="/wiki/%D1%8F%D0%B1%D0%BB%D0%BE%D0%BA%D0%BE#Russian" title=""></a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jbloko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc"><a href="/wiki/%E1%BC%84%CE%BC%CF%80%CE%B5%CE%BB%CE%BF%CF%82#Ancient_Greek" title=""></a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mpelos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote"></span><span class="mention-gloss">vine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote"></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=apple&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=apple&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">apple</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/apples#English" title="apples">apples</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href="/wiki/common" title="common">common</a>, <a href="/wiki/round" title="round">round</a> <a href="/wiki/fruit" title="fruit">fruit</a> produced by the <a href="/wiki/tree" title="tree">tree</a> <i><a href="/wiki/Malus_domestica" title="Malus domestica">Malus domestica</a></i>, cultivated in <a href="/wiki/temperate" title="temperate">temperate</a> climates. <span class="defdate">[from 9th c.]</span>
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><b>c. 1378</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Langland" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Langland">William Langland</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Piers_Plowman" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Piers Plowman">Piers Plowman</a></i>:
<dl><dd>I prayed pieres to pulle adown an <b>apple</b>.</dd></dl></li>

<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2013</b> October 28,  John Vallins,  Apples of concord, in  <cite>The Guardian</cite><sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.theguardian.com/environment/2013/oct/28/somerset-apples-of-concord">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Close by and under cover, I watched the juicing process. <b>Apples</b> were washed, then tipped, stalks and all, into the crusher and reduced to pulp.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>Any <a href="/wiki/fruit" title="fruit">fruit</a> or <a href="/wiki/vegetable" title="vegetable">vegetable</a>, or any other thing produced by a plant such as a <a href="/wiki/gall" title="gall">gall</a> or <a href="/wiki/cone" title="cone">cone</a>, especially if produced by a tree and similar to the fruit of <i><a href="/wiki/Malus_domestica" title="Malus domestica">Malus domestica</a></i>; also (with qualifying words) used to form the names of specific fruits such as <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/custard_apple#English" title="custard apple">custard apple</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/rose_apple#English" title="rose apple">rose apple</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/thorn_apple#English" title="thorn apple">thorn apple</a></i> etc. <span class="defdate">[from 9th c.]</span>
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><b>1585</b>, Richard Eden (translating a 1555 work by Peter Martyr), <i>Decades of the New World</i>, v:
<dl><dd>Venemous <b>apples</b> wherwith they poyson theyr arrows.</dd></dl></li>

<dl><dd>The fruit or <b>Apples</b> of Palm-trees.</dd></dl></li>

<dl><dd>This <b>apple</b> is called in high-Dutch, <span class="Latf" lang="de">Zybel</span>: in low-Dutch, <span class="Latf" lang="nl">Pijnappel</span>: in English, Pineapple, Clog, and Cone. <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> The whole cone or <b>apple</b> being boiled with fresh Horehound, saith <i>Galen</i>, <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="and afterwards boiled again with a little hony vntill the decoction be come to the thicknesse of honey,"></span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> maketh an excellent medicine for to clense the chest and lungs.</dd></dl></li>

<dl><dd>In Persia there grows a deadly tree, whose <b>Apples</b> are Poison, and present death.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1765</b>, Abraham Tucker, <i>The Light of Nature Pursued</i>, page 337:
<dl><dd>The fly injects her juices into the oak-leaf, to raise an <b>apple</b> for hatching her young.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1784</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/James_Cook" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:James Cook">James Cook</a>, <i>A Voyage to the Pacific Ocean</i>, II:
<dl><dd>Otaheite [] is remarkable for producing great quantities of that delicious fruit we called <b>apples</b>, which are found in none of the others, except Eimeo.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1800</b>, John Tuke,  <i>General View of the Agriculture of the North Riding of Yorkshire</i>, page 150:
<dl><dd>It is generally thought, that the curled topped potatoe proceeds from a neglect of raising fresh sorts from the <b>apple</b> or [potato-]seed.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1825</b>, Theodric Romeyn Beck, <i>Elements of Medical Jurisprudence</i>, 2nd edition, page 565:
<dl><dd><i>Hippomane mancinella.</i> (Manchineel-tree.) Dr. Peysonnel relates that a soldier, who was a slave with the Turks, eat some of the <b>apples</b> of this tree, and was soon seized with a swelling and pain of the abdomen.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1833</b>, Charles Williams, <i>The Vegetable World</i>, page 179:
<dl><dd>One kind of <b>apple</b> or gall, inhabited only by one grub, is hard and woody on the outside, resembling a little wooden ball, of a yellowish color, but internally it is of a soft, spongy texture.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1853</b>, Mrs. S. F. Cowper, <i>Country Rambles in England, Or, Journal of a Naturalist</i>, page 172:
<dl><dd>The cross-bill will have seeds from the <b>apple</b>, or cone of the firthe green-finch, seeds from the uplands, or door of barn, or rick-yard.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1889</b>, United States. Department of Agriculture, <i>Report of the Secretary of Agriculture</i>, page 376:
<dl><dd>The "<b>apple</b>" or gall usually forms a somewhat kidney-shaped excrescence, attached by a small base on the concave side, and varying in size from a half an inch to an inch and a half in length.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Something which resembles the fruit of <i><a href="/wiki/Malus_domestica" title="Malus domestica">Malus domestica</a></i>, such as a <a href="/wiki/globe" title="globe">globe</a>, <a href="/wiki/ball" title="ball">ball</a>, or <a href="/wiki/breast" title="breast">breast</a>.

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=apple&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Verb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">apple</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3|s|pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/apples#English" title="apples">apples</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/appling#English" title="appling">appling</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past|and|past|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/appled#English" title="appled">appled</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To become apple-like.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1992</b>,  Marilyn Strathern,  <cite>Reproducing the Future</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">One might say they have to be <b>appled</b>-up; varieties are selected for marketing which have the most apple-like qualities.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2004</b>,  Gregory David Roberts,  <cite>Shantaram: A Novel</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">He glanced at me, his cheeks <b>appled</b> in the impish grin I was learning to recognise as the clever under-side of his broad and gentle smile.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2007</b>,  Claudia D. Newcorn,  <cite>Crossover: Krisalys Chronicles of Feyree</cite>, page 35:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">A large smile <b>appled</b> his full cheeks as the four sprytes eagerly served themselves from the seeds and thinly sliced fruits.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b>,  Cynthia Robinson,  <cite>The Barbary Dogs</cite>, page 57:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">She smiled, and her cheeks <b>appled</b> up and her teeth were big and flat and her mouth was wide and spacious like an open invitation.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#obsolete" title="Appendix:Glossary">obsolete</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To form buds, bulbs, or fruit.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><b>1601</b> (1634), Philemon Holland (translator), <i>Pliny</i>, II, page 98:
<dl><dd>Either they floure, or they <b>apple</b> or els be ready to bring forth fruit.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1767</b>,  James Justice,  <cite>The British gardener's calendar</cite>, page 274:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">You may now sow upon moderate hot-beds, a few of the small Salad feeds, such as White Mustard, Rape, Cresses, and Cabbage Lettuces, and you may also sow upon other hot-beds, not to be drawn until they are pretty large and well <b>appled</b>, Radishes and Turnips, observing to sow them very thin, that the plants may have room to swell and grow;</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>1796</b> (1800), Charles Marshall, <i>Gardening</i>, page 245:
<dl><dd>The cabbage turnep is of two kinds; one <b>apples</b> above ground, and the other in it.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1807</b>,  <cite>The Complete Farmer</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Other cultivators, however, advise "that the seed collected from a few turnips thus transplanted, should be preserved and sown in drills, in order to raise plants for see for the general crop, drawing out all such as are weak and improper, leaving only those that are strong and which take the lead; and that when these have <b>appled</b> or formed bulbs, to again take out such as do not appear good and perfect, as by this means turnip seed may be procured, not only of a more vigorous nature, but which is capable of vegetating with less moisture and which produces stronger and more hardy plants.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/malic#English" title="malic">malic</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">ethnic slur</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/coconut#English" title="coconut">coconut</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/Oreo#English" title="Oreo">Oreo</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/banana#English" title="banana">banana</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/Twinkie#English" title="Twinkie">Twinkie</a></span></li></ul>
